              * * *  Maple Integration Test Results - 2011-06-08  * * *


Test file:  ExponentialFunctions/LogarithmFunctions.txt

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = x^2*ln(a*x^n)
  Optimal integral = -1/9*x^3*(n-3*ln(a*x^n))
  Maple integral   = 1/3*x^3*ln(x^n)+1/18*x^3*(6*ln(a)-3*I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)*csgn(I*a)*csgn(I*x^n)-3*I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^3+3*I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*x^n)+3*I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*a)-2*n)

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = x^3*ln(a*x^n)
  Optimal integral = -1/16*x^4*(n-4*ln(a*x^n))
  Maple integral   = 1/4*x^4*ln(x^n)+1/16*x^4*(4*ln(a)-2*I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)*csgn(I*a)*csgn(I*x^n)-2*I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^3+2*I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*x^n)+2*I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*a)-n)

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = ln(a*x^n)/x^2
  Optimal integral = (-ln(a*x^n)-n)/x
  Maple integral   = -1/x*ln(x^n)-1/2*(2*n+2*ln(a)-I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)*csgn(I*a)*csgn(I*x^n)-I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^3+I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*x^n)+I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*a))/x

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = ln(a*x^n)/x^3
  Optimal integral = 1/4*(-2*ln(a*x^n)-n)/x^2
  Maple integral   = -1/2/x^2*ln(x^n)-1/4*(n+2*ln(a)-I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)*csgn(I*a)*csgn(I*x^n)-I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^3+I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*x^n)+I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*a))/x^2

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = x^m*ln(a*x^n)
  Optimal integral = x^(1+m)*((1+m)*ln(a*x^n)-n)/(1+m)^2
  Maple integral   = 1/(1+m)*x*x^m*ln(x^n)-1/2*(-2*ln(a)-2*ln(a)*m+I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)*csgn(I*a)*csgn(I*x^n)+I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)*csgn(I*a)*csgn(I*x^n)*m+I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^3+I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^3*m-I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*x^n)-I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*x^n)*m-I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*a)-I*Pi*csgn(I*a*x^n)^2*csgn(I*a)*m+2*n)/(1+m)^2*x*x^m

Unable to integrate:
  Integrand        = x^3*ln(c*(a*x^n)^p)
  Optimal integral = -1/16*x^4*(n*p-4*ln(c*(a*x^n)^p))
  Maple integral   = int(x^3*ln(c*(a*x^n)^p),x)

Unable to integrate:
  Integrand        = x^m*ln(c*(a*x^n)^p)
  Optimal integral = ((1+m)*ln(c*(a*x^n)^p)-n*p)*x^(1+m)/(1+m)^2
  Maple integral   = int(x^m*ln(c*(a*x^n)^p),x)

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = 1/ln(a*x)
  Optimal integral = Li(a*x)/a
  Maple integral   = -1/a*Ei(1,-ln(a*x))
  Leafcounts = 8 13   8 13

Unable to integrate:
  Integrand        = x^m/ln(a*x)
  Optimal integral = x^(1+m)*(a*x)^(-1-m)*Ei((1+m)*ln(a*x))
  Maple integral   = int(x^m/ln(a*x),x)

Unable to integrate:
  Integrand        = 1/ln(a*x^n)
  Optimal integral = x*Ei(ln(a*x^n)/n)/n/((a*x^n)^(1/n))
  Maple integral   = int(1/ln(a*x^n),x)

Unable to integrate:
  Integrand        = x/ln(a*x^n)
  Optimal integral = x^2*Ei(2*ln(a*x^n)/n)/n/((a*x^n)^(2/n))

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = ln(c*x^n)/(a+b*x)^3
  Optimal integral = 1/2*(-n*(a+b*x)^2*ln(a+b*x)-ln(c*x^n)*a^2+(a+b*x)*n*(ln(x)*(a+b*x)+a))/a^2/b/(a+b*x)^2

Maple gives a simpler antiderivative!:
  Integrand        = ln(a*x)/(1-a*x)
  Optimal integral = polylog(2,1-a*x)/a
  Maple integral   = 1/a*dilog(a*x)
  Leafcounts = 12 8   0 0

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = x^3*ln(c*(a+b*x^2)^n)^3
